          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Saturday, August 17, 2013</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry'>
<a name='6815376553683990'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='http://otrbuffet.blogspot.com/2013/08/id-just-die-without-old-radio.html'>I'd just die without old radio</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content'>
The title, "I'd just die without old radio", was uttered to me yesterday. It was not tongue-in-cheek, but rather a true sentiment.&nbsp; I know this becuse the person telling me was my brother.<br />
<br />
Here's the short version of a very long story: recently, my long, lost brother knocked on my door.&nbsp; He needed help; worse, he was in a life or death situation (or at least, very close to it.)<br />
<br />
Needless to say, I took him in.&nbsp; Better yet, my relationship with my brother, which had been badly damaged over the years, has been repaired.<br />
<br />
I've always known my brother enjoyed old radio.&nbsp; I have no television at my house.&nbsp; What can one do for entertainment, especially right before bed?&nbsp; Well, listen to OTR, of course.<br />
<br />
I hooked him up a small iPod and 500 random shows.&nbsp; He loved it.&nbsp; Loved it so much that he now goes to bed early to listen to it.&nbsp; It so reminds me of when I was a young teen; I couldn't wait to get under the covers and listen to OTR.&nbsp; He basically told me this yesterday (he's almost 61 years old.)&nbsp; He told me that he'd die if something happened to the iPod or I took it away from him and he wouldn't be able to listen to OTR!&nbsp; He's hopelessly addicted and this is a GOOD addiction.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-footer'>
<div class='post-footer-line post-footer-line-1'><span class='post-author vcard'>

<h2>IMPORTANT OTR LINKS</h2>
<div class='widget-content'>
<ul>
<li><a href='http://1940s.org/'>1940's, The - The Greatest Generation</a></li>
<li><a href='http://www.supermanhomepage.com/radio/radio.php?topic=radio-reviews/radio-reviews'>Adventures of Superman radio plots and reviews (AWESOME!)</a></li>

Self-taught musician, I've been writing music since age 9 and can play over 30 instruments.</dd>

<!-- Start post reversal code -->
<script type='text/javascript'>
  var Blog1 = document.getElementById('Blog1');
  var postContainer = Blog1.childNodes[1];
  var first = postContainer.firstChild;
  var child = first.nextSibling;
  var childNext = null;
  var classes = '';

  var dateHeaders = false;
  while (child != null) {
    if (child.className == 'date-header') {
      dateHeaders = true;
      break;
    }
    child = child.nextSibling;
  }

  child = first.nextSibling;

  while (child != null) {
    if (child.className != null) {
      if (child.className.match('date-header') != null) {
        childNext = child.nextSibling;
        postContainer.insertBefore(child, first);
        first = child;
        child = childNext;
      } else if (child.className.match('post hentry') != null) {
        childNext = child.nextSibling;
        if (!dateHeaders) {
          postContainer.insertBefore(child, first);
          first = child;
        } else {
          postContainer.insertBefore(child, first.nextSibling);
        }
        child = childNext;
      } else {
        child = child.nextSibling;
      }
    } else {
      child = child.nextSibling;
    }
  }
</script>
